  `id_venta` varchar(20) NOT NULL,

  `cantidad` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `costo` varchar(20) NOT NULL
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COLLATE=utf8mb3_spanish_ci;
